  `no` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `history` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `place` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `substance` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,

  KEY `history_substances_history_foreign` (`history`),

  CONSTRAINT `history_substances_history_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`history`) REFERENCES `histories` (`no`),

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=733 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;
